migration squashing compliance through a comprehensive system involving multiple interconnected components:\\n\\n**1. Squash Migration Generator (django/core/management/commands/squashmigrations.py)**\\nThe `Command` class and its `handle()` method orchestrate the squash migration creation process. It loads the migration graph, identifies migrations to squash, collects their operations, optimizes them using `MigrationOptimizer`, and creates a new migration file with the `replaces` attribute listing all squashed migrations.\\n\\n**2. Replaced-Migrations Tracking (django/db/migrations/migration.py + django/db/migrations/recorder.py)**\\nThe base `Migration` class defines a `replaces` attribute (list of tuples) that tracks which migrations a squashed migration replaces. The `MigrationRecorder` class tracks applied migrations in the django_migrations database table. When a squashed migration is applied via the executor, it records both the squashed migration name AND the names of all individual replaced migrations (see `record_migration()` in executor.py).\\n\\n**3. Dependency Graph Validation After Squashing (django/db/migrations/graph.py)**\\nThe `MigrationGraph` class implements critical validation:\\n- `validate_consistency()`: Ensures no dummy nodes remain (references to non-existent migrations)\\n- `ensure_not_cyclic()`: Detects and rejects circular dependencies in the migration graph\\n- `remove_replaced_nodes()`: Removes replaced migration nodes and remaps dependencies to point to the replacement\\n- `remove_replacement_node()`: Inverse operation for handling partially applied squashed migrations\\n\\nThese methods are called during graph construction in `MigrationLoader.build_graph()`.\\n\\n**4. Squash Completeness Check (django/db/migrations/loader.py)**\\nThe `MigrationLoader` class implements sophisticated checks:\\n- `replace_migration()`: Processes each replacement migration, recursively handling nested squashes. Detects cyclical replacements via `replacements_progress` tracking and raises `CommandError` for cycles.\\n- `_resolve_replaced_migration_keys()`: Recursively resolves nested squashed migrations (squashes of squashes) to find all original migrations\\n- `all_replaced_applied()`: Checks if all original replaced migrations are marked as applied in the database\\n- `check_consistent_history()`: Validates that unapplied squashed migrations have all their replaced migrations either all applied or none applied (prevents partial application states)\\n\\nThe loader only includes a squashed migration in the main graph if either all or none of its replaced migrations are applied. If partially applied, it creates a dummy node and removes the squashed migration to prevent using an incomplete replacement.\\n\\n**5. Executor-Level Compliance (django/db/migrations/executor.py)**\\nThe `MigrationExecutor` class enforces compliance during migration execution:\\n- `migration_plan()`: Handles squashed migrations by rebuilding the graph without replacements if a target migration isn't found, allowing fallback to original migrations\\n- `record_migration()`: When recording a squashed migration as applied, it also records each of its replaced migrations individually\\n- `check_replacements()`: Called after every migration execution to mark squashed migrations as applied when all their replaced migrations are applied (handles the case where all replacements were applied before the squash was created)\\n\\nThis multi-layered approach ensures: (1) squashed migrations are properly generated with dependency tracking, (2) the migration graph remains consistent and acyclic, (3) circular dependencies in replacement chains are detected, (4) squashed migrations are only applied when all their replaced migrations can be properly tracked, and (5) database records accurately reflect both squashed and original migration states.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":831,"cache_read_input_tokens":72670,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":831},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b32949fb-2f57-4240-aa37-e63f08dc9de7","uuid":"32756d7b-fbe9-47d1-8966-daa378ecbff4"}
